</tr>
</table>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Booster-Layout.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Booster-Layout.jpg/200px-Booster-Layout.jpg" width="200" height="71" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Booster-Layout.jpg/300px-Booster-Layout.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Booster-Layout.jpg/400px-Booster-Layout.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5770" data-file-height="2058" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Booster-Layout.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A drawing for a booster engine for <a href="/wiki/Steam_locomotive" title="Steam locomotive">steam locomotives</a>. Engineering is applied to <a href="/wiki/Design" title="Design">design</a>, with emphasis on function and the utilization of mathematics and science.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Engineers use their knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Science" title="Science">science</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mathematics" title="Mathematics">mathematics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Logic" title="Logic">logic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Economics" title="Economics">economics</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Empirical_knowledge" class="mw-redirect" title="Empirical knowledge">appropriate experience</a> or <a href="/wiki/Tacit_knowledge" title="Tacit knowledge">tacit knowledge</a> to find suitable solutions to a problem. Creating an appropriate <a href="/wiki/Mathematical_model" title="Mathematical model">mathematical model</a> of a problem allows them to analyze it (sometimes definitively), and to test potential solutions.</p>
<p>Usually, multiple reasonable solutions exist, so engineers must evaluate the different <a href="/wiki/Design_choice" title="Design choice">design choices</a> on their merits and choose the solution that best meets their requirements. <a href="/wiki/Genrich_Altshuller" title="Genrich Altshuller">Genrich Altshuller</a>, after gathering statistics on a large number of <a href="/wiki/Patent" title="Patent">patents</a>, suggested that <a href="/wiki/Compromise" title="Compromise">compromises</a> are at the heart of "<a href="/wiki/Level_of_invention" title="Level of invention">low-level</a>" engineering designs, while at a higher level the best design is one which eliminates the core contradiction causing the problem.</p>
<p>Engineers typically attempt to predict how well their designs will perform to their specifications prior to full-scale production. They use, among other things: <a href="/wiki/Prototype" title="Prototype">prototypes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scale_model" title="Scale model">scale models</a>, <a href="/wiki/Simulation" title="Simulation">simulations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Destructive_testing" title="Destructive testing">destructive tests</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nondestructive_testing" title="Nondestructive testing">nondestructive tests</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Stress_testing" title="Stress testing">stress tests</a>. Testing ensures that products will perform as expected.</p>
<p>Engineers take on the responsibility of producing designs that will perform as well as expected and will not cause unintended harm to the public at large. Engineers typically include a <a href="/wiki/Factor_of_safety" title="Factor of safety">factor of safety</a> in their designs to reduce the risk of unexpected failure. However, the greater the safety factor, the less efficient the design may be.</p>
<p>The study of failed products is known as <a href="/wiki/Forensic_engineering" title="Forensic engineering">forensic engineering</a> and can help the <a href="/wiki/Product_design" title="Product design">product designer</a> in evaluating his or her design in the light of real conditions. The discipline is of greatest value after disasters, such as <a href="/wiki/Bridge_collapse" class="mw-redirect" title="Bridge collapse">bridge collapses</a>, when careful analysis is needed to establish the cause or causes of the failure.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Computer_use">Computer use</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Computer use">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:227px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CFD_Shuttle.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/CFD_Shuttle.jpg/225px-CFD_Shuttle.jpg" width="225" height="169" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/CFD_Shuttle.jpg/338px-CFD_Shuttle.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/CFD_Shuttle.jpg/450px-CFD_Shuttle.jpg 2x" data-file-width="516" data-file-height="387" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CFD_Shuttle.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A computer simulation of high velocity air flow around a <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_orbiter" title="Space Shuttle orbiter">Space Shuttle orbiter</a> during re-entry. Solutions to the flow require <a href="/wiki/Finite_element_method" title="Finite element method">modelling</a> of the combined effects of <a href="/wiki/Navier%E2%80%93Stokes_equations" title="Navier–Stokes equations">fluid flow</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Heat_equation" title="Heat equation">heat equations</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As with all modern scientific and technological endeavors, computers and software play an increasingly important role. As well as the typical business <a href="/wiki/Application_software" title="Application software">application software</a> there are a number of computer aided applications (<a href="/wiki/Computer-aided_technologies" title="Computer-aided technologies">computer-aided technologies</a>) specifically for engineering. Computers can be used to generate models of fundamental physical processes, which can be solved using <a href="/wiki/Numerical_method" title="Numerical method">numerical methods</a>.</p>
<p>One of the most widely used <a href="/wiki/Design_tool" title="Design tool">design tools</a> in the profession is <a href="/wiki/Computer-aided_design" title="Computer-aided design">computer-aided design</a> (CAD) software like <a href="/wiki/CATIA" title="CATIA">CATIA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Autodesk_Inventor" title="Autodesk Inventor">Autodesk Inventor</a>, DSS <a href="/wiki/SolidWorks" title="SolidWorks">SolidWorks</a> or <a href="/wiki/Pro_Engineer" class="mw-redirect" title="Pro Engineer">Pro Engineer</a> which enables engineers to create 3D models, 2D drawings, and schematics of their designs. CAD together with <a href="/wiki/Digital_mockup" title="Digital mockup">digital mockup</a> (DMU) and <a href="/wiki/Computer-aided_engineering" title="Computer-aided engineering">CAE</a> software such as <a href="/wiki/Finite_element_method" title="Finite element method">finite element method analysis</a> or <a href="/wiki/Analytic_element_method" title="Analytic element method">analytic element method</a> allows engineers to create models of designs that can be analyzed without having to make expensive and time-consuming physical prototypes.</p>
<p>These allow products and components to be checked for flaws; assess fit and assembly; study ergonomics; and to analyze static and dynamic characteristics of systems such as stresses, temperatures, electromagnetic emissions, electrical currents and voltages, digital logic levels, fluid flows, and kinematics. Access and distribution of all this information is generally organized with the use of <a href="/wiki/Product_data_management" title="Product data management">product data management</a> software.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></p>
<p>There are also many tools to support specific engineering tasks such as <a href="/wiki/Computer-aided_manufacturing" title="Computer-aided manufacturing">computer-aided manufacturing</a> (CAM) software to generate <a href="/wiki/CNC" class="mw-redirect" title="CNC">CNC</a> machining instructions; <a href="/wiki/Manufacturing_process_management" title="Manufacturing process management">manufacturing process management</a> software for production engineering; <a href="/wiki/Electronic_design_automation" title="Electronic design automation">EDA</a> for <a href="/wiki/Printed_circuit_board" title="Printed circuit board">printed circuit board</a> (PCB) and circuit <a href="/wiki/Schematic" title="Schematic">schematics</a> for electronic engineers; <a href="/wiki/Maintenance,_repair,_and_operations" title="Maintenance, repair, and operations">MRO</a> applications for maintenance management; and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Architecture,_engineering_and_construction&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Architecture, engineering and construction (page does not exist)">AEC</a> software for civil engineering.</p>
<p>In recent years the use of computer software to aid the development of goods has collectively come to be known as <a href="/wiki/Product_lifecycle_management" class="mw-redirect" title="Product lifecycle management">product lifecycle management</a> (PLM).<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Social_context">Social context</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Social context">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Original_research" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/40px-Ambox_important.svg.png" width="40" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/60px-Ambox_important.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/80px-Ambox_important.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="40" data-file-height="40" /></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>possibly contains <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research" title="Wikipedia:No original research">original research</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit">improve it</a> by <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verifying</a> the claims made and adding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources#Inline_citations" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">inline citations</a>. Statements consisting only of original research should be removed.</span> <small><i>(July 2010)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg/200px-Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg" width="200" height="267" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg/300px-Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg/400px-Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1704" data-file-height="2272" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kismet_robot_20051016.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Robotic" class="mw-redirect" title="Robotic">Robotic</a> <a href="/wiki/Kismet_(robot)" title="Kismet (robot)">Kismet</a> can produce a range of facial expressions.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The engineering profession engages in a wide range of activities, from large collaboration at the societal level, and also smaller individual projects. Almost all engineering projects are obligated to some sort of financing agency: a company, a set of investors, or a government. The few types of engineering that are minimally constrained by such issues are <i><a href="/wiki/Pro_bono" title="Pro bono">pro bono</a></i> engineering and <a href="/wiki/Open_design" title="Open design">open-design</a> engineering.</p>
<p>By its very nature engineering has interconnections with society, culture and human behavior. Every product or construction used by modern society is influenced by engineering. The results of engineering activity influence changes to the environment, society and economies, and its application brings with it a responsibility and public safety. Many <a href="/wiki/Engineering_society" class="mw-redirect" title="Engineering society">engineering societies</a> have established codes of practice and <a href="/wiki/Engineering_ethics" title="Engineering ethics">codes of ethics</a> to guide members and inform the public at large.</p>
<p>Engineering projects can be subject to controversy. Examples from different engineering disciplines include the development of <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapon" title="Nuclear weapon">nuclear weapons</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Three_Gorges_Dam" title="Three Gorges Dam">Three Gorges Dam</a>, the design and use of <a href="/wiki/Sport_utility_vehicle" title="Sport utility vehicle">sport utility vehicles</a> and the extraction of <a href="/wiki/Fuel_oil" title="Fuel oil">oil</a>. In response, some western engineering companies have enacted serious <a href="/wiki/Corporate_social_responsibility" title="Corporate social responsibility">corporate and social responsibility</a> policies.</p>
<p>Engineering is a key driver of innovation and human development. Sub-Saharan Africa, in particular, has a very small engineering capacity which results in many African nations being unable to develop crucial infrastructure without outside aid.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The attainment of many of the <a href="/wiki/Millennium_Development_Goals" title="Millennium Development Goals">Millennium Development Goals</a> requires the achievement of sufficient engineering capacity to develop infrastructure and sustainable technological development.<sup id="cite_ref-MDG_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MDG-28">[28]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:ElementBlack2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ElementBlack2.jpg/250px-ElementBlack2.jpg" width="250" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ElementBlack2.jpg/375px-ElementBlack2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/ElementBlack2.jpg/500px-ElementBlack2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="1000" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:ElementBlack2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Radar, <a href="/wiki/GPS" class="mw-redirect" title="GPS">GPS</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lidar" title="Lidar">lidar</a>, ... are all combined to provide proper navigation and <a href="/wiki/Obstacle_avoidance" title="Obstacle avoidance">obstacle avoidance</a> (vehicle developed for 2007 <a href="/wiki/DARPA_Urban_Challenge" class="mw-redirect" title="DARPA Urban Challenge">DARPA Urban Challenge</a>)</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>All overseas development and relief NGOs make considerable use of engineers to apply solutions in disaster and development scenarios. A number of charitable organizations aim to use engineering directly for the good of mankind:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Engineers_Without_Borders" title="Engineers Without Borders">Engineers Without Borders</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Engineers_Against_Poverty" title="Engineers Against Poverty">Engineers Against Poverty</a></li>
<li>Registered Engineers for Disaster Relief</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Engineers_for_a_Sustainable_World" title="Engineers for a Sustainable World">Engineers for a Sustainable World</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Engineering_for_Change" title="Engineering for Change">Engineering for Change</a></li>
<li>Engineering Ministries International<sup id="cite_ref-EMI_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EMI-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<p>Engineering companies in many established economies are facing significant challenges with regard to the number of professional engineers being trained, compared with the number retiring. This problem is very prominent in the UK where engineering has a poor image and low status.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> There are many negative economic and political issues that this can cause, as well as ethical issues<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> It is widely agreed that the engineering profession faces an "image crisis",<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> rather than it being fundamentally an unattractive career. Much work is needed to avoid huge problems in the UK and other western economies.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships_with_other_disciplines">Relationships with other disciplines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Relationships with other disciplines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Science">Science</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Science">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<blockquote class="templatequote">
<p><i>Scientists study the world as it is; engineers create the world that has never been.</i></p>
<div class="templatequotecite"><cite>— <a href="/wiki/Theodore_von_K%C3%A1rm%C3%A1n" title="Theodore von Kármán">Theodore von Kármán</a><sup id="cite_ref-Caltech_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Caltech-33">[33]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ryschkewitsch_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ryschkewitsch-34">[34]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></cite></div>
</blockquote>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg/300px-Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg" width="300" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg/450px-Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/7d/Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="294" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Technician_inside_NIF_target_chamber.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Engineers, scientists and technicians at work on target positioner inside <a href="/wiki/National_Ignition_Facility" title="National Ignition Facility">National Ignition Facility</a> (NIF) target chamber</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>There exists an overlap between the sciences and engineering practice; in engineering, one applies science. Both areas of endeavor rely on accurate observation of materials and phenomena. Both use mathematics and classification criteria to analyze and communicate observations.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Scientists may also have to complete engineering tasks, such as designing experimental apparatus or building prototypes. Conversely, in the process of developing technology engineers sometimes find themselves exploring new phenomena, thus becoming, for the moment, scientists or more precisely "engineering scientists".<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>In the book <i><a href="/wiki/What_Engineers_Know_and_How_They_Know_It" title="What Engineers Know and How They Know It">What Engineers Know and How They Know It</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-vincenti_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vincenti-36">[36]</a></sup> Walter Vincenti asserts that engineering research has a character different from that of scientific research. First, it often deals with areas in which the basic <a href="/wiki/Physics" title="Physics">physics</a> or <a href="/wiki/Chemistry" title="Chemistry">chemistry</a> are well understood, but the problems themselves are too complex to solve in an exact manner.</p>
<p>There is a "real and important" difference between engineering and physics as similar to any science field has to do with technology.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> Physics is an exploratory science that seeks knowledge of principles while Engineering uses knowledge for practical applications of principles. The former equates an understanding into a mathematical principle while the latter measures variables involved and creates technology.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> For technology, physics is an auxiliary and in a way technology is considered as applied physics.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> Though Physics and Engineering are interrelated it doesn't mean a Physicist is sufficient where an Engineer is required. For this mobility, a physicist to work as an engineer requires additional and relevant specialized training.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> Physicists and engineers engage in different lines of work.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> But PhD physicists who specialize in sectors of <a href="/wiki/Engineering_physics" title="Engineering physics">technology</a> and <a href="/wiki/Applied_physics" title="Applied physics">applied science</a> are titled as Technology officer, R&amp;D Engineers and System Engineers.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> Though as an engineer, role of a physicist is limited.<sup id="cite_ref-NOC2111_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NOC2111-46">[46]</a></sup> Physicists in their field, work in theoretical analysis and experimental research.<sup id="cite_ref-NCS_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NCS-47">[47]</a></sup></p>
<p>An example of this is the use of numerical approximations to the <a href="/wiki/Navier%E2%80%93Stokes_equations" title="Navier–Stokes equations">Navier–Stokes equations</a> to describe aerodynamic flow over an aircraft, or the use of <a href="/wiki/Fatigue_(material)" title="Fatigue (material)">Miner's rule</a> to calculate fatigue damage. Second, engineering research employs many semi-<a href="/wiki/Empirical_methods" class="mw-redirect" title="Empirical methods">empirical methods</a> that are foreign to pure scientific research, one example being the method of parameter variation.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>As stated by Fung <i>et al.</i> in the revision to the classic engineering text <i>Foundations of Solid Mechanics</i>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Engineering is quite different from science. Scientists try to understand nature. Engineers try to make things that do not exist in nature. Engineers stress innovation and invention. To embody an invention the engineer must put his idea in concrete terms, and design something that people can use. That something can be a complex system, device, a gadget, a material, a method, a computing program, an innovative experiment, a new solution to a problem, or an improvement on what already exists. Since a design has to be realistic and functional, it must have its geometry, dimensions, and characteristics data defined. In the past engineers working on new designs found that they did not have all the required information to make design decisions. Most often, they were limited by insufficient scientific knowledge. Thus they studied mathematics, physics, chemistry, biology and mechanics. Often they had to add to the sciences relevant to their profession. Thus engineering sciences were born.<sup id="cite_ref-Fung_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fung-48">[48]</a></sup></p>
</blockquote>
<p>Although engineering solutions make use of scientific principles, engineers must also take into account safety, efficiency, economy, reliability, and constructability or ease of fabrication as well as the environment, ethical and legal considerations such as patent infringement or liability in the case of failure of the solution.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Medicine_and_biology">Medicine and biology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Medicine and biology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:227px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg/225px-Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg" width="225" height="351" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg/338px-Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg/450px-Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg 2x" data-file-width="740" data-file-height="1153" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Leonardo_da_Vinci_-_presumed_self-portrait_-_WGA12798.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci" title="Leonardo da Vinci">Leonardo da Vinci</a>, seen here in a self-portrait, has been described as the epitome of the artist/engineer.<sup id="cite_ref-Bjerklie.2C_David_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bjerklie.2C_David-49">[49]</a></sup> He is also known for his studies on <a href="/wiki/Human_anatomy" class="mw-redirect" title="Human anatomy">human anatomy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Physiology" title="Physiology">physiology</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The study of the human body, albeit from different directions and for different purposes, is an important common link between medicine and some engineering disciplines. <a href="/wiki/Medicine" title="Medicine">Medicine</a> aims to sustain, repair, enhance and even replace functions of the <a href="/wiki/Human_body" title="Human body">human body</a>, if necessary, through the use of <a href="/wiki/Technology" title="Technology">technology</a>.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:GFP_Mice_01.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/GFP_Mice_01.jpg/220px-GFP_Mice_01.jpg" width="220" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/GFP_Mice_01.jpg/330px-GFP_Mice_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/GFP_Mice_01.jpg/440px-GFP_Mice_01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1005" data-file-height="784" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:GFP_Mice_01.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Genetically engineered mice expressing <a href="/wiki/Green_fluorescent_protein" title="Green fluorescent protein">green fluorescent protein</a>, which glows green under blue light. The central mouse is <a href="/wiki/Wild-type" class="mw-redirect" title="Wild-type">wild-type</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Modern medicine can replace several of the body's functions through the use of artificial organs and can significantly alter the function of the human body through artificial devices such as, for example, <a href="/wiki/Brain_implant" title="Brain implant">brain implants</a> and <a href="/wiki/Artificial_pacemaker" class="mw-redirect" title="Artificial pacemaker">pacemakers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Boston_U_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Boston_U-50">[50]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-IEEE_foreign_parts_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IEEE_foreign_parts-51">[51]</a></sup> The fields of <a href="/wiki/Bionics" title="Bionics">bionics</a> and medical bionics are dedicated to the study of synthetic implants pertaining to natural systems.</p>
<p>Conversely, some engineering disciplines view the human body as a biological machine worth studying and are dedicated to emulating many of its functions by replacing <a href="/wiki/Biology" title="Biology">biology</a> with technology. This has led to fields such as <a href="/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neural_networks" class="mw-redirect" title="Neural networks">neural networks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fuzzy_logic" title="Fuzzy logic">fuzzy logic</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Robot" title="Robot">robotics</a>. There are also substantial interdisciplinary interactions between engineering and medicine.<sup id="cite_ref-IME_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IME-52">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-IEEE_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IEEE-53">[53]</a></sup></p>
<p>Both fields provide solutions to real world problems. This often requires moving forward before phenomena are completely understood in a more rigorous scientific sense and therefore experimentation and <a href="/wiki/Empirical" class="mw-redirect" title="Empirical">empirical</a> knowledge is an integral part of both.</p>
<p>Medicine, in part, studies the function of the human body. The human body, as a biological machine, has many functions that can be modeled using engineering methods.<sup id="cite_ref-Royal_Academy_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Royal_Academy-54">[54]</a></sup></p>
<p>The heart for example functions much like a pump,<sup id="cite_ref-Science_Museum_of_Minnesota_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Science_Museum_of_Minnesota-55">[55]</a></sup> the skeleton is like a linked structure with levers,<sup id="cite_ref-Minnesota_State_University_emuseum_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Minnesota_State_University_emuseum-56">[56]</a></sup> the brain produces <a href="/wiki/Signal_(electrical_engineering)" title="Signal (electrical engineering)">electrical signals</a> etc.<sup id="cite_ref-UC_Berkeley_News_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UC_Berkeley_News-57">[57]</a></sup> These similarities as well as the increasing importance and application of engineering principles in medicine, led to the development of the field of <a href="/wiki/Biomedical_engineering" title="Biomedical engineering">biomedical engineering</a> that uses concepts developed in both disciplines.</p>
<p>Newly emerging branches of science, such as <a href="/wiki/Systems_biology" title="Systems biology">systems biology</a>, are adapting analytical tools traditionally used for engineering, such as systems modeling and computational analysis, to the description of biological systems.<sup id="cite_ref-Royal_Academy_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Royal_Academy-54">[54]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Art">Art</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Art">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There are connections between engineering and art;<sup id="cite_ref-Lehigh_University_project_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lehigh_University_project-58">[58]</a></sup> they are direct in some fields, for example, <a href="/wiki/Architecture" title="Architecture">architecture</a>, <a href="/wiki/Landscape_architecture" title="Landscape architecture">landscape architecture</a> and <a href="/wiki/Industrial_design" title="Industrial design">industrial design</a> (even to the extent that these disciplines may sometimes be included in a university's <a href="/wiki/Faculty_(division)" title="Faculty (division)">Faculty</a> of Engineering); and indirect in others.<sup id="cite_ref-Lehigh_University_project_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lehigh_University_project-58">[58]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-National_Science_Foundation:The_Art_of_Engineering_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-National_Science_Foundation:The_Art_of_Engineering-59">[59]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MIT_World:The_Art_of_Engineering_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MIT_World:The_Art_of_Engineering-60">[60]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-University_of_Texas_at_Dallas_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-University_of_Texas_at_Dallas-61">[61]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Art_Institute_of_Chicago" title="Art Institute of Chicago">Art Institute of Chicago</a>, for instance, held an exhibition about the art of <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s aerospace design.<sup id="cite_ref-NASA_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NASA-62">[62]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Maillart" title="Robert Maillart">Robert Maillart</a>'s bridge design is perceived by some to have been deliberately artistic.<sup id="cite_ref-Princeton_U_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Princeton_U-63">[63]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/University_of_South_Florida" title="University of South Florida">University of South Florida</a>, an engineering professor, through a grant with the <a href="/wiki/National_Science_Foundation" title="National Science Foundation">National Science Foundation</a>, has developed a course that connects art and engineering.<sup id="cite_ref-National_Science_Foundation:The_Art_of_Engineering_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-National_Science_Foundation:The_Art_of_Engineering-59">[59]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chief_engineer_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chief_engineer-64">[64]</a></sup></p>
<p>Among famous historical figures, <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci" title="Leonardo da Vinci">Leonardo da Vinci</a> is a well-known <a href="/wiki/Renaissance" title="Renaissance">Renaissance</a> artist and engineer, and a prime example of the nexus between art and engineering.<sup id="cite_ref-Bjerklie.2C_David_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bjerklie.2C_David-49">[49]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Drew_U_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Drew_U-65">[65]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Business_Engineering_and_Engineering_Management">Business Engineering and Engineering Management</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Business Engineering and Engineering Management">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Business_Engineering" class="mw-redirect" title="Business Engineering">Business Engineering</a> deals with the relationship between professional engineering, IT systems, business administration and <a href="/wiki/Change_management" title="Change management">change management</a>. <a href="/wiki/Engineering_management" title="Engineering management">Engineering management</a> or "Management engineering" is a specialized field of <a href="/wiki/Management" title="Management">management</a> concerned with engineering practice or the engineering industry sector. The demand for management-focused engineers (or from the opposite perspective, managers with an understanding of engineering), has resulted in the development of specialized engineering management degrees that develop the knowledge and skills needed for these roles. During an engineering management course, students will develop <a href="/wiki/Industrial_engineering" title="Industrial engineering">industrial engineering</a> skills, knowledge, and expertise, alongside knowledge of business administration, management techniques, and strategic thinking. Engineers specializing in change management must have in-depth knowledge of the application of <a href="/wiki/Industrial_and_organizational_psychology" title="Industrial and organizational psychology">industrial and organizational psychology</a> principles and methods. Professional engineers often train as <a href="/wiki/Certified_management_consultant" title="Certified management consultant">certified management consultants</a> in the very specialized field of <a href="/wiki/Management_consulting" title="Management consulting">management consulting</a> applied to engineering practice or the engineering sector. This work often deals with large scale complex <a href="/wiki/Business_transformation" title="Business transformation">business transformation</a> or <a href="/wiki/Business_process_management" title="Business process management">Business process management</a> initiatives in aerospace and defence, automotive, oil and gas, machinery, pharmaceutical, food and beverage, electrical &amp; electronics, power distribution &amp; generation, utilities and transportation systems. This combination of technical engineering practice, management consulting practice, industry sector knowledge, and change management expertise enables professional engineers who are also qualified as management consultants to lead major business transformation initiatives. These initiatives are typically sponsored by C-level executives.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_fields">Other fields</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Other fields">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In other fields not associated with <a href="/wiki/Regulation_and_licensure_in_engineering" title="Regulation and licensure in engineering">professional engineering</a> the word "engineer" and or "engineering" has been adapted to mean design, develop, contrive, manipulate, implement an outcome.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> In <a href="/wiki/Political_science" title="Political science">political science</a>, the term <i>engineering</i> has been borrowed for the study of the subjects of <a href="/wiki/Social_engineering_(political_science)" title="Social engineering (political science)">social engineering</a> and <a href="/wiki/Political_engineering" title="Political engineering">political engineering</a>, which deal with forming <a href="/wiki/Political_structure" title="Political structure">political</a> and <a href="/wiki/Social_structure" title="Social structure">social structures</a> using engineering methodology coupled with <a href="/wiki/Political_science" title="Political science">political science</a> principles. <a href="/wiki/Financial_engineering" title="Financial engineering">Financial engineering</a> has similarly borrowed the term.</p>

<th style="padding:0.1em"><a href="/wiki/Chemistry" title="Chemistry">Chemistry</a></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="padding:0 0.1em 0.4em">
<div class="hlist">
<ul>

<li id="cite_note-Bjerklie.2C_David-49"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Bjerklie.2C_David_49-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Bjerklie.2C_David_49-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Bjerklie, David.
